# Expanded View Table 3	
# All sRNA-mRNA interactions recovered from replicate RNase E CLASH experiments.		
# Column 1	seq_ID: Unique sequence identifier for the hybrid read		
# Column 2	RNA1_feature: Feature mapping to the first half of the hybrid read. The format is chromosome | common name | systematic name | RNA class		
# Column 3 	RNA1_start: The starting coordinate for the first mapped read half		
# Column 4	RNA2_end: The end coordinate for the first mapped read half		
# Column 5	RNA2_feature: Feature mapping to the second half of the hybrid read. Format as RNA1_feature		
# Column 6	RNA2_start: The starting coordinate for the second mapped read half		
# Column 7	RNA2_end: The end coordinate for the second mapped read half		
# Column 8	count_total: Total number of unique reads mapping to RNA-RNA interaction		
# Column 9	count_last_clustering: Number of interactions overlapping in replicate dataset; no overlap = 1		
# Column 10	two_way_merged: If the RNA-RNA interaction was recovered in both the RNA1-RNA2 and RNA2-RNA1 orientations two_way_merged=1; otherwise two_way_merged=0		
# Column 11     ∆G: Gibbs free energy of interaction (kcal/mol)
# Column 12	literature: lit=Y if the sRNA-mRNA interaction has been described in the literature
# Column 13	Hfq_overlap_target: If the target (non-EcOnc) hybrid half overlaps a Hfq-binding site (read from Hfq-CRAC expt; Tree et al Mol Cell 2014), Hfq_overlap_RNA1=1; else 0
# Column 14	target_oligo(A): If non-genomic oligo adenylation was detected within 10t of the 3’ end of the target, target_oligo(A)=1; else = 0
# Column 15	E2: If the interaction was detected in replicate datasets, E2 = 1; else 0
# Column 16	count: count_total divided by 10. For calculating the score
# Column 17	score: Sum of Hfq_overlap_target, target_oligo(A), E2, count, two_way_merged
# Column 18	sequence: Sequence of the read
# Column 19	FDR: Benjamini–Hochberg corrected p-value. NB: No FDR or connection score calculated for hybrids halves < 100nt from each other. 
# Column 20	Connection score: ratio of hybrids to non-hybrid reads calculated as per Lu et al. Cell 2016 ( hybrids/sqrt(non-hybrids_A*non-hybrids_B) )
